        <script type="text/javascript">
         function searchSubmit(form) {
 		    var search = encodeURIComponent(form.w.value);
 		    if (search === "") {
 		        search = "*";
 		    }
 			document.activeElement.blur();
 			window.location = "http://search.supercheapauto.com.au/search?w=" + search;
 			return false;
 		}
        </script>
